cause and effect reasoning 

[
  {
    "id": 1,
    "question": "Statement I: The central bank significantly increased the repo rate. \nStatement II: Retail loan EMIs for home and auto buyers have gone up.",
    "options": {
      "A": "Statement I is the cause and Statement II is its effect.",
      "B": "Statement II is the cause and Statement I is its effect.",
      "C": "Both statements are effects of independent causes.",
      "D": "Both statements are effects of a common cause."
    },
    "answer": "A",
    "explanation": "When the central bank increases interest rates (repo rate), commercial banks pass this cost to consumers, causing EMIs to rise."
  },
  {
    "id": 2,
    "question": "Statement I: Most flights out of the city were canceled this morning. \nStatement II: All schools and colleges in the city declared an emergency holiday today.",
    "options": {

coding-decoding


[
  {
    "id": 1,
    "question": "In a certain code language, 'WATER' is written as 'YCVGT'. How is 'FIRE' written in that code?",
    "options": {
      "A": "HKTG",
      "B": "GLSF",
      "C": "EKQD",
      "D": "DJPC"
    },
    "answer": "A",
    "explanation": "Each letter in the word is shifted forward by 2 positions in the English alphabet. F(+2)=H, I(+2)=K, R(+2)=T, E(+2)=G."
  },
  {
    "id": 2,
    "question": "If 'GO' is coded as 32 and 'SHE' is coded as 49, then how will 'SOME' be coded?",
    "options": {
      "A": "56",
      "B": "58",
      "C": "62",
      "D": "64"
    },
    "answer": "A",
    "explanation": "The numbers represent the sum of the reverse alphabetical positions of the letters. G(20) + O(12) = 32. S(8) + H(19) + E(22) = 49. S(8) + O(12) + M(14) + E(22) = 56."
  },
  {
    "id": 3,
    "question": "In a certain code, 'BRAIN' is written as 'CQBJO'. How is 'MAKER' written in that code?",
    "options": {
      "A": "LZJDQ",
      "B": "NBLFS",
      "C": "NZLDS",
      "D": "NBKFS"
